<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привлечь.html>привле́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privléčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привлекать.html>привлека́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attract, to draw <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">arouse interest</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***привод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>привод</a> (17393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, since the 19th century. Perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Antrieb</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́д</a><sup>*</sup></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prívod</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privód<sup>*</sup></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вода</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́да</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>привода́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́ды</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приводо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́дов</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приводно́й</b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Alternative, non-professional-only usage.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drive, driving gear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ремённый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">remjónnyj <b>prívod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">belt drive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кулачко́вый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kulačkóvyj <b>prívod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cam gear/drive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цепной.html>цепно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cepnój <b>prívod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">chain drive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручной.html>ручно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ručnój <b>prívod</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hand gear</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>при́вод</a></b> компакт-ди́сков</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prívod</b> kompakt-dískov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">CD-ROM drive</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>приво́дов</a></b>)
</p>

***приводиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приводиться.html>приводи́ться</a> (11125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приводиться.html>приводи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">привести́сь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to happen to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative and infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have the occasion to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative and infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">приво́лье</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privólʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***привстававший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привставать.html>привстава́вший</a> (27419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привстать.html>привста́ть</a> (7156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привстать.html>привста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privstátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привставать.html>привстава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to half-rise</li>
<li>to rise, stand up
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привстать.html>привста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цыпочки.html>цы́почки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> лучше <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происходящий.html>происходя́щее</a>. (He stood on tiptoe to see better what was happening.)</dd></dl></li></ol>

***привыкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привыкать.html>привыка́ть</a> (5329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привыкнуть.html>привы́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privýknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привыкать.html>привыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привыкнуть.html>привы́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get used to, to get accustomed to</li></ol>

***привыкший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привыкший.html>привы́кший</a> (975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязать.html>привяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязаться.html>привяза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privjazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязываться.html>привя́зываться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to become/get/be attached <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>не́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязаться.html>привяза́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on óčenʹ k néj <b>privjazálsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has become very (much) attached to her</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attach oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a> кака́я-то <a href = vnd.unilang:собачонок.html>собачо́нка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязаться.html>привяза́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na úlice kakája-to sobačónka <b>privjazálasʹ</b> k nemú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a stray dog attached itself to him in the street</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bother, to pester
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязаться.html>привяза́лся</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što ty k nemú <b>privjazálsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">why are you bothering him?; why don't you leave him alone?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязать.html>привяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зка</a> (29427)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязать.html>привяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privjázka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tying, attaching</li>
<li>linkage, affixment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privjázka</b> pó vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">timing <i>(to)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privjázka</b> cen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pegging of prices</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> binding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязка.html>привя́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privjázka</b> dánnyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">data binding</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***привязывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привязывать.html>привя́зывать</a> (10726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязать.html>привяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязывать.html>привя́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privjázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязать.html>привяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to attach, to fasten, to tether
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:восток.html>восто́ке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрец.html>мудрецы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́т</a>: «<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аллах.html>алла́ха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надеяться.html>наде́йся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верблюд.html>верблю́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:привязывать.html>привя́зывай</a></b>!».</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na Vostóke mudrecý govorját: “Na Alláxa nadéjsja, a verbljúda <b>privjázyvaj</b>!”.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sages in the Orient say: "Rely on Allah but tie up your camel!".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to win over, to attach</li></ol>

***привязываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привязываться.html>привя́зываться</a> (24031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязывать.html>привя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязываться.html>привя́зываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privjázyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязаться.html>привяза́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become/get/be attached <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attach oneself <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bother, to pester</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привязывать.html>привя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">privjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
